## Brand Guidelines

### 2021

**Logo Information:**

- Details about the logo usage, types, and placements, including guidelines for clearance area and co-branding scenarios.

**Color Information:**

- Information on color palettes, including primary and accent colors, digital-optimized values, and principles for consistent use.

**Typography Information:**

- Ericsson Hilda typeface usage, hierarchy, and guidelines for readability including font weights and tracking adjustments.

**Imagery Photography:**

- Photography style and image treatment rules in specific contexts (e.g., social media avatars, roll-ups).

**Spacing Layout:**

- Grid system specifications and layout guidelines for digital and print contexts, including exceptions and scalability.

**Brand Voice:**

- Tone guidelines including messaging consistency and placement of partner/co-branding messages.

**Notes:**

- General supporting notes and reminders about the guidelines, and connection to Ericsson Brand House for detailed reference.
